## 2. L0_CONSTITUTIONAL (Core, Types, Safety) (100 Directives)

- **Criticality:** DAL-A / CRITICAL
- **STAMP Mapping:** `SC-CRYPTO-142` (Unsafe Control Action / Process Model Flaw)
- **Information Metrics:** H(source)=7.002, I(source;target)=2.631, Loss=4.371 bits
- **FMEA Analysis:**

  - *Effect:* Data corruption enters the system at the lowest boundary via `Int`. Shannon entropy of state space exceeds safe bounds (H=7.00 bits).
